  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Pivotal NAVAL-1 study of Nana-val in Epstein-Barr virus-positive (EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">) lymphoma open at 70 sites globally; update on first lymphoma subtype that may advance from Stage 1 to Stage 2 expected in the first half of 2023</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Completed initial enrollment into the fourth dose level in the dose escalation part of the Phase 1b/2 trial of Nana-val in advanced EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> solid tumors</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Data from the complete dose escalation part of the Phase 1b/2 trial of Nana-val in advanced EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> solid tumors expected in 2023</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Received orphan drug designation (ODD) from the European Commission for Nana-val for the treatment of diffuse large B-cell lymphoma; sixth ODD globally and the second in Europe</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Cash, cash equivalents and investments of $91.0 million as of December 31, 2022; anticipated cash runway into late 2024</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">San Diego, March 13, 2023 &#x2013; Viracta Therapeutics, Inc. (Nasdaq: VIRX), a precision oncology company focused on the treatment and prevention of virus-associated cancers that impact patients worldwide, today announced financial results for the fourth quarter and full year 2022 and provided an update on recent corporate developments.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;Over the past months we made important progress towards our goal of developing Nana-val as a tumor agnostic therapy for patients with difficult-to-treat EBV-associated cancers,&#x201d; said Mark Rothera, President and Chief Executive Officer of Viracta. &#x201c;The latest data from our solid tumor trial showed a confirmed partial response and no dose limiting toxicities through three of five planned dose levels in patients with recurrent or metastatic nasopharyngeal carcinoma. We look forward to reporting data from the full dose escalation part of the trial, selecting our recommended Phase 2 dose, initiating the Phase 2 nasopharyngeal carcinoma expansion cohort and evaluating Nana-val in additional EBV-positive solid tumors later this year. Our pivotal NAVAL-1 trial site footprint continues to grow as we seek to advance multiple EBV-positive lymphoma subtypes into Stage 2 of this global study. With these anticipated milestones ahead of us and a cash runway into late 2024, we believe Viracta is well-positioned to generate value for patients and shareholders over the coming months.&#x201d;</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Program Highlights and Anticipated Milestones</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Pivotal NAVAL-1 trial of Nana-val in relapsed/refractory (R/R) EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">+ </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">lymphoma</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NAVAL-1 continues to make strong progress with 70 sites open for enrollment globally and medical science liaisons deployed in all key territories. Continued expansion of the study footprint is anticipated in 2023.</font></div></div>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">An update on NAVAL-1&#x2019;s first lymphoma subtype that may advance from Stage 1 to Stage 2 is anticipated in the first half of 2023.</font></div></div>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Additional update(s) on other NAVAL-1 lymphoma subtype(s) are expected throughout 2023. </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">		Page | </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">1</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 1b/2 trial of Nana-val in patients with recurrent/metastatic (R/M) EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">nasopharyngeal carcinoma (NPC) and other advanced EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> solid tumors</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Preliminary safety and efficacy data from the first three dose levels of the Phase 1b dose escalation part of the trial were presented at the European Society for Medical Oncology Immuno-Oncology (ESMO-IO) Conference in December 2022. Data showed that Nana-val was well tolerated with no dose limiting toxicities (DLTs) reported.</font></div></div>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Partial response (PR) confirmed at the third dose level of the Phase 1b dose escalation part of the trial. Initial enrollment into the fourth dose level is complete. </font></div></div>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Complete Phase 1b dose escalation data and selection of the recommended Phase 2 dose (RP2D) are expected in 2023.</font></div></div>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Initiation of the trial&#x2019;s Phase 2 randomized expansion cohort designed to evaluate Nana-val at the RP2D with or without pembrolizumab in patients with R/M EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NPC is expected in the second half of 2023.</font></div></div>
  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Initiation of the trial&#x2019;s exploratory Phase 1b expansion cohort designed to evaluate Nana-val at the RP2D in patients with other advanced EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> solid tumors is expected in the second half of 2023. </font></div></div>

  <div style="text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:2.667%;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:2.667%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net loss &#x2013; </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net loss was approximately $10.3 million, or $0.27 per share (basic and diluted) for the quarter ended December 31, 2022, compared to a net loss of $11.4 million or $0.31 per share (basic and diluted) for the same period in 2021. Net loss was approximately $49.2 million, or $1.30 per share (basic and diluted) for the year ended December 31, 2022, compared to a net loss of $114.8 million or $3.60 per share (basic and diluted) for the same period in 2021.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About NAVAL-1</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NAVAL-1 (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NCT05011058</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">) is a global, multicenter trial of Nana-val in R/R EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> lymphoma. The trial employs a Simon two-stage design where participants are enrolled into six indication cohorts based on EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">lymphoma subtype in Stage 1.  If a pre-specified activity threshold is reached within a lymphoma subtype in Stage 1 (n=10), additional patients will be enrolled in Stage 2 for a total of 21 patients. EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+ </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">lymphoma subtypes demonstrating promising activity in Stage 2 may be further expanded following discussion with regulators to potentially support registration.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About the Phase 1b/2 Trial of Nana-val in R/M EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> NPC and Other EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Solid Tumors</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">This Phase 1b/2 trial (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">NCT05166577</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">) is an open-label, multinational trial evaluating Nana-val alone and in combination with pembrolizumab. The Phase 1b dose escalation part is designed to evaluate safety and to determine the RP2D of Nana-val in patients with R/M EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> NPC. In Phase 2, up to sixty patients with R/M EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> NPC will be randomized to receive Nana-val at the RP2D with or without pembrolizumab to evaluate safety, overall response rate, and potential pharmacodynamic markers. Additionally, patients with other advanced EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> solid tumors will be enrolled to receive Nana-val at the RP2D in a Phase 1b dose expansion cohort.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About Nana-val (Nanatinostat and Valganciclovir)</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Nanatinostat is an orally available histone deacetylase (HDAC) inhibitor being developed by Viracta. Nanatinostat is selective for specific isoforms of Class I HDACs, which are key to inducing viral genes that are epigenetically silenced in Epstein-Barr virus (EBV)-associated malignancies. Nanatinostat is currently being investigated in combination with the antiviral agent valganciclovir as an all-oral combination therapy, Nana-val, in various subtypes of EBV-associated malignancies. Ongoing trials include a pivotal, global, multicenter, open-label Phase 2 basket trial in multiple subtypes of relapsed/refractory EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+ </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">lymphoma (NAVAL-1) as well as a multinational Phase 1b/2 trial in patients with EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> recurrent or metastatic nasopharyngeal carcinoma and other EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> solid tumors.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About Viracta Therapeutics, Inc.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Viracta is a precision oncology company focused on the treatment and prevention of virus-associated cancers that impact patients worldwide. Viracta&#x2019;s lead product candidate is an all-oral combination therapy of its proprietary investigational drug, nanatinostat, and the antiviral agent valganciclovir (collectively referred to as Nana-val).</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">		Page | </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">3</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Nana-val is currently being evaluated in multiple ongoing clinical trials, including a pivotal, global, multicenter, open-label Phase 2 basket trial for the treatment of multiple subtypes of relapsed/refractory Epstein-Barr virus-positive (EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">) lymphoma (NAVAL-1), as well as a multinational, open-label Phase 1b/2 trial for the treatment of EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">recurrent or metastatic nasopharyngeal carcinoma and other EBV</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">+</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> solid tumors. Viracta is also pursuing the application of its &#x201c;</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Kick and Kill&#x201d;</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> approach in other virus-related cancers.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(33,37,41,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">For additional information please visit </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">www.viracta.com</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(33,37,41,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font><font style="color:rgba(33,37,41,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
